14/03/2023, 20:05 - KilllerrrrrğŸ¦‹â¤ï¸â€ğŸ©¹: import java.util.Scanner;
public class Quadratic
{
	public static void main(String[]args)
	{
		int a,b,c;
		double root1,root2;
		System.out.println("Enter the cofficients ");
		Scanner in =new Scanner (System.in);
		a=in.nextInt();
		b=in.nextInt();
		c=in.nextInt();
		double d=b*b-4*a*c;
		System.out.println("determinant="+d);
		if(d>0)
		{
			root1=(-b+Math.sqrt(d))/(2*a);
			root2=(-b-Math.sqrt(d))/(2*a);
			System.out.println("The roots are real and distinct");
			System.out.format("root1=%.2f and root2=%.2f",root1,root2);
		}
		else if (d==0)
		{
			root1=root2=-b/(2*a);
			System.out.println("The roots are real and equal");
			System.out.format ("root1=root2=%.2f;",root1);
		}
		else 
		{
			double real =-b/(2*a);
			double imaginary = Math.sqrt(-d)/(2*a);
			System.out.println("The roots are imaginary");
			System.out.format("root1=%2.f+2fi",real,imaginary );
			System.out.format("\nroot2=%2.f-%.2fi",real,imaginary);
		}
	}
}

20/04/2023, 17:12 - ^aceâ™¤: *multiple edges*:(also called parallel edges or a multi-edge), are, in an undirected graph, two or more edges that are incident to the same two vertices, or in a directed graph, two or more edges with both the same tail vertex and the same head vertex.
20/04/2023, 17:13 - ^aceâ™¤: *directed graph*: is a data structure that stores data in vertices or nodes and these nodes or vertices are connected and also directed by edges (one vertex is directed towards another vertex through an edge) that may have some weight. Directed graph is also called a digraph or directed network.
20/04/2023, 17:14 - ^aceâ™¤: *Multi Graph* :If there are numerous edges between a pair of vertices in a graph G= (V, E), the graph is referred to as a multigraph. There are no self-loops in a Multigraph.
20/04/2023, 17:14 - ^aceâ™¤: *complete graph*:is a simple undirected graph in which every pair of distinct vertices is connected by a unique edge

elif x<0 and y<0:
    print("it lies in 3rd quadrant") 
else:
    print("it does not lie in any quadrant")

23/06/2023, 10:41 - KilllerrrrrğŸ¦‹â¤ï¸â€ğŸ©¹: #include <iostream>
using namespace std;

class Graph {
   private:
  bool** adjMatrix;
  int numVertices;

   public:
  // Initialize the matrix to zero
  Graph(int numVertices) {
    this->numVertices = numVertices;
    adjMatrix = new bool*[numVertices];
    for (int i = 0; i < numVertices; i++) {
      adjMatrix[i] = new bool[numVertices];
      for (int j = 0; j < numVertices; j++)
        adjMatrix[i][j] = false;
    }
  }

  // Add edges
  void addEdge(int i, int j) {
    adjMatrix[i][j] = true;
    adjMatrix[j][i] = true;
  }

  // Remove edges
  void removeEdge(int i, int j) {
    adjMatrix[i][j] = false;
    adjMatrix[j][i] = false;
  }

  // Print the martix
  void toString() {
    for (int i = 0; i < numVertices; i++) {
      cout << i << " : ";
      for (int j = 0; j < numVertices; j++)
        cout << adjMatrix[i][j] << " ";
      cout << "\n";
    }
  }

  ~Graph() {
    for (int i = 0; i < numVertices; i++)
      delete[] adjMatrix[i];
    delete[] adjMatrix;
  }
};

int main() {
  Graph g(4);

  g.addEdge(1, 2);
  g.addEdge(0, 2);
  g.addEdge(1, 2);
  g.addEdge(2, 0);
  g.addEdge(2, 3);

  g.toString();
}

19/07/2023, 10:38 - ^aceâ™¤: Lipid-Based Soap Advantages


User
Advantages of lipids based on soap

ChatGPT
Lipids are a class of biomolecules that include fats, oils, waxes, and phospholipids. When lipids combine with a base (such as sodium hydroxide or potassium hydroxide), they form soap. Here are some advantages of using lipids-based soaps:

Biodegradability: Lipid-based soaps are biodegradable, meaning they can break down naturally in the environment. This is an essential advantage over some synthetic detergents that can persist in the environment and cause ecological harm.

Mildness on the skin: Soaps made from lipids tend to be gentle on the skin, making them suitable for people with sensitive or easily irritated skin. They are less likely to cause allergic reactions compared to harsher chemical detergents.

Natural origin: Lipid-based soaps are often derived from natural sources like plant oils (e.g., coconut oil, olive oil) or animal fats. Many people prefer using products with natural origins due to concerns about chemicals and synthetic additives.

Versatility: Lipid-based soaps have a wide range of applications. They can be used for personal hygiene, cleaning, laundry, and various household chores, making them versatile and practical.

Cleaning effectiveness: Soaps made from lipids are effective at removing dirt, grease, and oil from various surfaces, including skin and fabrics. They have good emulsifying properties, which help in dispersing oil and dirt particles.

Eco-friendly production: The production process for lipid-based soaps typically involves fewer harsh chemicals and energy-intensive processes compared to synthetic detergents. This can lead to a lower environmental impact during manufacturing.

Renewability: Many lipids used in soap production, such as vegetable oils, can be derived from renewable sources, making them a more sustainable choice compared to petroleum-based alternatives.

Safe disposal: Lipid-based soaps do not introduce harmful chemicals into wastewater, making them safer for the environment when washed down the drain.

Cost-effective: Lipid-based soaps can be cost-effective, especially when they are produced on a larger scale. The availability of raw materials and relatively simple production processes contribute to their affordability.

Despite these advantages, it's essential to note that lipids-based soaps also have some limitations. For instance, they may not perform as effectively in hard water, which can lead to soap scum formation. Additionally, the biodegradability of soap depends on the specific lipid used, the formulation, and other additives included. As with any product, it's essential to consider the entire lifecycle and environmental impact to make informed choices.

Mildness on the skin: Gentle and suitable for sensitive skin, minimizing allergic reactions.

19/07/2023, 10:50 - ^aceâ™¤: Biodiesel is a renewable and environmentally friendly alternative to conventional diesel fuel. It is a type of biofuel made from renewable resources, primarily plant oils (such as soybean, canola, or palm oil) and animal fats (like tallow or used cooking oil). The production process involves transesterification, where the triglycerides in the oils and fats are reacted with an alcohol (usually methanol) and a catalyst (such as sodium hydroxide) to yield biodiesel and glycerin.

Advantages of Biodiesel:

Renewable Energy Source: Biodiesel is derived from renewable resources, such as crops and waste cooking oil, which can be replenished, making it a sustainable energy option.

Lower Greenhouse Gas Emissions: Biodiesel generally emits fewer greenhouse gases, including carbon dioxide, compared to conventional diesel, contributing to reduced carbon footprints.

Biodegradability: Biodiesel is biodegradable, which means it breaks down more readily in the environment than petroleum-based diesel, reducing the potential for soil and water pollution.

Improved Lubricity: Biodiesel has better lubricating properties than conventional diesel, which can extend the lifespan of diesel engines and reduce wear on critical components.

Safer Handling: Biodiesel has a higher flashpoint and lower toxicity than conventional diesel, making it safer to handle and transport.

Potential for Local Production: Biodiesel can be produced locally, using locally available feedstocks, reducing dependence on foreign oil and providing economic benefits to local communities.

Disadvantages of Biodiesel:

Land Use Concerns: The production of biodiesel requires significant land resources, which may lead to deforestation, habitat destruction, and competition with food crops, potentially affecting food prices and availability.

Feedstock Competition: The demand for biodiesel feedstocks can lead to competition with food production, resulting in concerns about food security and higher prices for certain agricultural products.

Energy Intensive Production: The process of converting feedstocks into biodiesel can be energy-intensive, which may offset some of the environmental benefits if not sourced sustainably.

Cold Weather Performance: Biodiesel can have poor cold weather performance compared to conventional diesel, leading to potential issues with gelling or clogging of fuel lines in cold climates.

Fuel Stability: Biodiesel tends to have lower oxidative stability, which means it can degrade more quickly than conventional diesel, potentially leading to fuel quality issues over time.

Nitrogen Oxide (NOx) Emissions: In certain engine types, biodiesel may lead to slightly higher NOx emissions, which can contribute to air pollution and smog formation.

In conclusion, biodiesel offers several advantages as a renewable and cleaner alternative to conventional diesel. However, its widespread adoption faces challenges related to land use, feedstock competition, and energy-intensive production. Careful consideration of sustainable feedstock sourcing and technological advancements will be crucial to fully realize the benefits of biodiesel while minimizing its drawbacks.

23/09/2023, 15:43 - ^aceâ™¤: from PyPDF2 import PdfWriter, PdfReader

num = int(input("Enter page number you want to combine from multiple documents: "))

# Open the input PDF files
pdf1 = open('ISE2021Scheme.pdf', 'rb')
pdf2 = open('python syllabius.pdf', 'rb')

pdf_writer = PdfWriter()

# Read the specified page from the first PDF
pdf1_reader = PdfReader(pdf1)
page = pdf1_reader.pages[num - 1]
pdf_writer.add_page(page)

# Read the specified page from the second PDF
pdf2_reader = PdfReader(pdf2)
page = pdf2_reader.pages[num - 1]
pdf_writer.add_page(page)

# Close the input PDF files
pdf1.close()
pdf2.close()

# Write the combined PDF to an output file
with open('output.pdf', 'wb') as output:
    pdf_writer.write(output)

print("Combined PDF saved as 'output.pdf'")

AI has a wide range of applications, including autonomous vehicles, virtual assistants, recommendation systems, and even in healthcare for diagnosing diseases. 30/12/2023, 16:09 - ^aceâ™¤: Sure, here are a few examples of problem-solving agents:
â—Chess-playing AI: These agents use algorithms and heuristics to explore possible moves, predict future states, and select the best moves to win the game.

â—Pathfinding Algorithms: Agents like Dijkstra's algorithm or A* search algorithm navigate through graphs or maps to find the shortest path between two points, commonly used in GPS systems or game development.

â—Medical Diagnosis Systems: These agents analyze symptoms and medical history to suggest possible diseases or conditions, aiding healthcare professionals in making accurate diagnoses.

â—Robotics Control Systems: Agents that control robots to perform tasks in various environments, such as assembly line robots in manufacturing or autonomous vehicles navigating city streets.

â—Natural Language Processing (NLP) Chatbots: Agents capable of understanding and generating human language to answer queries, provide information, or assist with various tasks like customer service or information retrieval.

â—Scheduling and Planning Systems: Agents that optimize schedules, resource allocation, or project timelines, like in logistics, project management, or airline scheduling.
30/12/2023, 16:14 - ^aceâ™¤: Certainly! Problem-solving agents are entities designed to navigate through a series of states in an environment to reach a desirable goal state. These agents employ various strategies to solve problems effectively. Here's a more detailed explanation:

â—State Representation: Agents perceive the current state of the problem. This state could be represented using different formalisms, such as graphs, logical expressions, or other data structures depending on the nature of the problem.

â—Problem Formulation: The agent defines the problem by specifying the initial state, actions available, transition model (how actions change the state), goal test (conditions to check if the goal is achieved), and path cost (if applicable).

â—Search Algorithms: Agents employ search algorithms to traverse through the state space and find a sequence of actions that lead from the initial state to the goal state. These algorithms could be uninformed (e.g., breadth-first search, depth-first search) or informed/heuristic-based (e.g., A* search, iterative deepening).

â—Heuristics and Knowledge: In some cases, agents use domain-specific knowledge or heuristics to guide the search more efficiently. Heuristics provide estimates about the desirability of different states based on problem-specific information.

â—Goal Achievement: Agents iteratively apply actions based on the search strategy, transitioning between states until they reach a state that satisfies the goal test.
30/12/2023, 16:15 - ^aceâ™¤: *properties of problem-solving*:

â—Solvability: The problem has a finite number of possible states and can be solved using search algorithms like breadth-first search or depth-first search.

â—Optimality: It's possible to find the optimal solution by exploring all possible combinations, ensuring the safety of the missionaries while minimizing the number of boat trips.

â—Completeness: Given a finite state space, a solution will always exist and can be found using systematic search strategies.

â—Adaptability: Agents can modify their approach based on the state of the problem, ensuring that they don't violate the constraints.

â—Efficiency: Algorithms can be optimized to reduce unnecessary exploration of the state space, making the search more efficient.
30/12/2023, 16:40 - ^aceâ™¤: Problem-solving agents are entities that perceive their environment, formulate problems, search for solutions, and execute actions to achieve goals or resolve issues. These agents operate in dynamic environments where the state might change, requiring them to adapt their strategies.

01/01/2024, 23:24 - ^aceâ™¤: Accept State:
An accept state (also known as a final state or an accepting state) is a designated state within the finite automaton that signifies that the machine has successfully processed the entire input string and recognizes it as part of the language or pattern the automaton is designed to accept. When the finite automaton reaches an accept state after processing the entire input string, it indicates that the input string complies with the defined criteria or rules of the automaton.

Reject State:
Conversely, a reject state (also known as a non-final state or a non-accepting state) is any state that does not signify the successful acceptance of the input string according to the rules defined by the automaton. If the finite automaton ends up in a reject state after processing the entire input string, it indicates that the string does not meet the criteria or pattern recognized by the automaton, and thus, it is rejected.

Î´: is a transition function that maps a state and an input to a new state.
q0: is the initial state of the automaton.
F: is a set of accepting states.

03/01/2024, 05:30 - ^aceâ™¤: Integrity constraints are a set of rules. It is used to maintain the quality of information.
Integrity constraints ensure that the data insertion, updating, and other processes have to be performed in such a way that data integrity is not affected.
Thus, integrity constraint is used to guard against accidental damage to the database.

28/01/2024, 17:26 - ^aceâ™¤: Regular expressions describe patterns of strings, while finite automata are abstract machines that can recognize or generate strings based on a given pattern. 


Here are some other differences between regular expressions and finite automata:

*Purpose:* Regular expressions are a formal notation for generating patterns, while finite automata are used to recognize patterns.


*Complexity:* Finite automata can handle more complex patterns than regular expressions.


*Efficiency:* Finite automata can be more efficient when it comes to matching strings.


*Flexibility:* Regular expressions are typically less powerful and flexible than finite automata.


*Input:* Finite automata take the string of symbols as input and transform its state accordingly.


*Output:* Regular expressions are strings on Î£, which means they will consist only with input alphabets. 


Any regular expression can be converted into an equivalent finite automaton, and vice versa.

28/01/2024, 20:33 - ^aceâ™¤: 1st

Finite automata and regular expressions are both formalisms used in theoretical computer science to describe languages. Here's a brief differentiation:

Nature of Representation:

Finite Automata: Represents languages through states and transitions between states. It consists of a finite set of states, an alphabet of symbols, transitions based on input symbols, and designated initial and accepting states.
Regular Expressions: Represents languages through concise and expressive string patterns. It uses operators like concatenation, union, and closure to define patterns.
Expressiveness:

Finite Automata: Less expressive compared to regular expressions. It can recognize regular languages, but it may require more states and transitions for complex patterns.
Regular Expressions: Highly expressive and concise. They provide a compact way to describe regular languages and patterns.
Formalism vs. Notation:

Finite Automata: Focuses on the formalism of states and transitions. The emphasis is on the structure and behavior of the automaton.
Regular Expressions: Primarily a notation for describing patterns. It defines languages using a combination of symbols and operators.
Compactness:

Finite Automata: May require a larger number of states for certain languages, leading to a less compact representation.
Regular Expressions: Typically more concise, offering a compact way to represent patterns.
Operational vs. Declarative:

Finite Automata: Defines languages operationally, specifying the step-by-step transitions from one state to another based on input symbols.

Regular Expressions: Defines languages declaratively, specifying the overall pattern without detailing the step-by-step process of recognition.

(explain the regulations of tokens and specify them)
28/01/2024, 21:06 - ^aceâ™¤: In compiler design, the term "token" refers to the smallest unit of a programming language. The regulation of tokens involves defining rules and patterns to recognize and categorize these units during the lexical analysis phase. Here are some key regulations related to tokens:

1. *Character Set*: Define the allowable characters in the programming language. This includes letters, digits, symbols, and whitespace.

2. *Lexemes and Patterns*: Specify the lexemes, which are the basic units of syntax like keywords, identifiers, operators, and literals. Associate each lexeme with a corresponding pattern to identify its structure.

3. *Keywords*: List and define reserved words that have a special meaning in the language. These words cannot be used as identifiers.

4. *Identifiers*: Establish rules for forming valid identifiers, such as starting with a letter, allowing letters and digits, and avoiding reserved words.

5. *Operators*: Enumerate the operators in the language and define their associativity and precedence. Specify any special characters or combinations that represent operators.

6. *Literals*: Define the syntax for constants, such as numeric literals, string literals, and character literals. Specify how to represent these values in the source code.

7. *Comments*: Specify the syntax for comments and define how the compiler should treat them. Comments are ignored during compilation but are essential for code documentation.

8. *Whitespace and Formatting*: Define the significance of whitespace characters and how the compiler should handle indentation, line breaks, and other formatting aspects.

9. *Delimiters*: Identify special characters or sequences used to mark the beginning or end of blocks, statements, or other program constructs.

10. *Escape Sequences*: If applicable, specify how escape sequences in string literals should be interpreted.

Regulating tokens is crucial for creating a lexer that can effectively analyze the source code, break it into tokens, and pass them to the next phase of compilation for further processing.

03/03/2024, 23:45 - ^aceâ™¤: The ID is a triple (q, w, Î±), where:
q: The current state of the control unit
w: The unread part of the input string
Î³: The current contents of the PDA stack 
The leftmost symbol of the stack indicates the top of the stack, and the bottom is at the right end. 
For example, the instantaneous description for the string "aabb" is:
(q0, aabb, Z0)
(q0, abb, aZ0)
(q0, bb, aaZ0)
(q1, b, aZ0)
(q1, Î», Z0)
(q2, Î», Î») 

(ID EXAMPLE)

09/06/2024, 22:46 - ^aceâ™¤: import cv2
from cvzone.HandTrackingModule import HandDetector
import numpy as np
import math
import time
cap = cv2.VideoCapture(0)
detector = HandDetector(maxHands=1)
offset = 20
imgSize = 300
folder = "Data/C"
counter = 0
while True:
    success, img = cap.read()
    hands, img = detector.findHands(img)
    if hands:
        hand = hands[0]
        x, y, w, h = hand['bbox']
        imgWhite = np.ones((imgSize, imgSize, 3), np.uint8) * 255
        imgCrop = img[y - offset:y + h + offset, x - offset:x + w + offset]
        imgCropShape = imgCrop.shape
        aspectRatio = h / w
        if aspectRatio > 1:
            k = imgSize / h
            wCal = math.ceil(k * w)
            imgResize = cv2.resize(imgCrop, (wCal, imgSize))
            imgResizeShape = imgResize.shape
            wGap = math.ceil((imgSize - wCal) / 2)
            imgWhite[:, wGap:wCal + wGap] = imgResize
        else:
            k = imgSize / w
            hCal = math.ceil(k * h)
            imgResize = cv2.resize(imgCrop, (imgSize, hCal))
            imgResizeShape = imgResize.shape
            hGap = math.ceil((imgSize - hCal) / 2)
            imgWhite[hGap:hCal + hGap, :] = imgResize
        cv2.imshow("ImageCrop", imgCrop)
        cv2.imshow("ImageWhite", imgWhite)
    cv2.imshow("Image", img)
    key = cv2.waitKey(1)
    if key == ord("s"):
        counter += 1
        cv2.imwrite(f'{folder}/Image_{time.time()}.jpg',imgWhite)
        print(counter)

Note that the legacy SavedModel format is not supported by `load_model()` in Keras 3. In order to reload a TensorFlow SavedModel as an inference-only layer in Keras 3, use `keras.layers.TFSMLayer(Model/keras_model_h5, call_endpoint='serving_default')` (note that your `call_endpoint` might have a different name).

28/07/2024, 13:05 - KilllerrrrrğŸ¦‹â¤ï¸â€ğŸ©¹: def calculate_mex(arr):
    arr_set = set(arr)
    mex = 0
    while mex in arr_set:
        mex += 1
    return mex

def minimum_removals_to_change_mex(arr):
    original_mex = calculate_mex(arr)
    mex_count = arr.count(original_mex)

    # If the original MEX is 0, it can't be changed by definition of the problem
    if original_mex == 0:
        return -2

    # Check if we can change the MEX by removing all occurrences of the original MEX value
    if mex_count > 0:
        return mex_count

    # If all elements from 0 to original_mex-1 are present
    # Check for the first element missing in 0 to original_mex-1
    for i in range(original_mex):
        if arr.count(i) == 0:
            return -2

    # If all elements from 0 to original_mex-1 are present, we need to remove one of these elements
    return 1

# Reading input
I = int(input().strip())
A = list(map(int, input().strip().split()))

# Calculating the result
result = minimum_removals_to_change_mex(A)

# Printing the output
print(result)

void main() {
  runApp(const FigmaToCodeApp());
}

class FigmaToCodeApp extends StatelessWidget {
  const FigmaToCodeApp({super.key});

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return MaterialApp(
      theme: ThemeData.dark().copyWith(
        scaffoldBackgroundColor: const Color.fromARGB(255, 18, 32, 47),
      ),
      home: const OnboardingScreen(),
    );
  }
}

class OnboardingScreen extends StatefulWidget {
  const OnboardingScreen({super.key});

  @override
  _OnboardingScreenState createState() => _OnboardingScreenState();
}

class _OnboardingScreenState extends State<OnboardingScreen> {
  final PageController _pageController = PageController();
  int _currentPage = 0;

  void _onPageChanged(int page) {
    setState(() {
      _currentPage = page;
    });
  }

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return Scaffold(
      body: PageView(
        controller: _pageController,
        onPageChanged: _onPageChanged,
        children: [
          Frame112(),
          LoginPage(), // Redirect to LoginPage when sliding is complete
        ],
      ),
    );
  }
}

class Frame112 extends StatelessWidget {
  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return Column(
      children: [
        Container(
          width: double.infinity,
          height: MediaQuery.of(context).size.height,
          padding: const EdgeInsets.only(
            top: 100,
            left: 20,
            right: 20,
          ),
          clipBehavior: Clip.antiAlias,
          decoration: const BoxDecoration(
            gradient: LinearGradient(
              begin: Alignment(0.00, -1.00),
              end: Alignment(0, 1),
              colors: [Color(0xFF117AEE), Color(0xFFBAD7F7)],
            ),
          ),
          child: Column(
            mainAxisSize: MainAxisSize.min,
            mainAxisAlignment: MainAxisAlignment.center,
            crossAxisAlignment: CrossAxisAlignment.center,
            children: [
              Container(
                width: 140,
                height: 139,
                decoration: ShapeDecoration(
                  image: const DecorationImage(
                    image: AssetImage("assets/logo.png"), // Use the local image
                    fit: BoxFit.cover,
                  ),
                  shape: RoundedRectangleBorder(
                    side: BorderSide(
                      width: 1,
                      color: Colors.black.withOpacity(0),
                    ),
                    borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(100),
                  ),
                  shadows: const [
                    BoxShadow(
                      color: Color(0x4C000000),
                      blurRadius: 4,
                      offset: Offset(0, 4),
                      spreadRadius: 0,
                    ),
                    BoxShadow(
                      color: Color(0x26000000),
                      blurRadius: 12,
                      offset: Offset(0, 8),
                      spreadRadius: 6,
                    )
                  ],
                ),
              ),
              const SizedBox(height: 20),
              const Text(
                "Welcome to Digitome!",
                style: TextStyle(fontSize: 24, color: Colors.white),
              ),
            ],
          ),
        ),
      ],
    );
  }
}

01/11/2024, 21:35 - KilllerrrrrğŸ¦‹â¤ï¸â€ğŸ©¹: import 'package:flutter/material.dart';
import 'home.dart'; // Import your HomePage
import 'package:firebase_auth/firebase_auth.dart';

class SignUpPage extends StatefulWidget {
  @override
  _SignUpPageState createState() => _SignUpPageState();
}

class _SignUpPageState extends State<SignUpPage> {
  final TextEditingController _employeeIdController = TextEditingController();
  final TextEditingController _emailController = TextEditingController();
  final TextEditingController _passwordController = TextEditingController();
  final TextEditingController _confirmPasswordController = TextEditingController();

  bool _isPasswordVisible = false;
  bool _isConfirmPasswordVisible = false;

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return Scaffold(
      backgroundColor: const Color(0xFFB9D7F6), // Background color gradient end
      body: SingleChildScrollView(
        child: Column(
          children: [
            Container(
              width: double.infinity,
              height: 846,
              decoration: BoxDecoration(
                gradient: LinearGradient(
                  begin: Alignment(0.00, -1.00),
                  end: Alignment(0, 1),
                  colors: [Color(0xFF107AED), Color(0xFFB9D7F6)], // Gradient from the original
                ),
                borderRadius: BorderRadius.only(
                  bottomLeft: Radius.circular(40),
                  bottomRight: Radius.circular(40),
                ),
              ),
              child: Padding(
                padding: const EdgeInsets.symmetric(horizontal: 34.0), // Use consistent padding
                child: Column(
                  children: [
                    SizedBox(height: 135), // Space from the top
                    // Logo Placeholder Image
                    Container(
                      width: 165,
                      height: 145,
                      decoration: BoxDecoration(
                        image: DecorationImage(
                          image: AssetImage("assets/images/logo1.png"),
                          fit: BoxFit.cover,
                        ),
                      ),
                    ),
                    SizedBox(height: 20),
                    // Sign Up Text
                    Text(
                      'SIGN UP',
                      style: TextStyle(
                        color: Colors.black,
                        fontSize: 32,
                        fontFamily: 'Roboto',
                        fontWeight: FontWeight.bold,
                        letterSpacing: 1.5,
                      ),
                    ),
                    SizedBox(height: 40),
                    // Employee ID input field
                    _buildInputField(
                      controller: _employeeIdController,
                      icon: "assets/images/Vector.png",
                      placeholder: 'EMPLOYEE ID',
                      isPassword: false,
                    ),
                    SizedBox(height: 20),
                    // Email input field
                    _buildInputField(
                      controller: _emailController,
                      icon: "assets/images/email.png",
                      placeholder: 'EMAIL',
                      isPassword: false,
                    ),
                    SizedBox(height: 20),
                    // Password input field
                    _buildInputField(
                      controller: _passwordController,
                      icon: "assets/images/lock.png",
                      placeholder: 'PASSWORD',
                      isPassword: true,
                      isVisible: _isPasswordVisible,
                      toggleVisibility: () {
                        setState(() {
                          _isPasswordVisible = !_isPasswordVisible;
                        });
                      },
                    ),
                    SizedBox(height: 20),
                    // Confirm Password input field
                    _buildInputField(
                      controller: _confirmPasswordController,
                      icon: "assets/images/lock.png",
                      placeholder: 'CONFIRM PASSWORD',
                      isPassword: true,
                      isVisible: _isConfirmPasswordVisible,
                      toggleVisibility: () {
                        setState(() {
                          _isConfirmPasswordVisible = !_isConfirmPasswordVisible;
                        });
                      },
                    ),
                    SizedBox(height: 40), // Space before the button
                    // Sign Up button
                    GestureDetector(
                      onTap: () async {
                        if (_passwordController.text.trim() ==
                            _confirmPasswordController.text.trim()) {
                          try {
                            // Create user with Firebase
                            UserCredential userCredential = await FirebaseAuth.instance.createUserWithEmailAndPassword(
                              email: _emailController.text.trim(),
                              password: _passwordController.text.trim(),
                            );
                            // Navigate to HomePage
                            Navigator.pushReplacement(
                              context,
                              MaterialPageRoute(builder: (context) => HomePage()),
                            );
                          } on FirebaseAuthException catch (e) {
                            // Handle error
                            ScaffoldMessenger.of(context).showSnackBar(
                              SnackBar(content: Text(e.message ?? 'Sign up failed')),
                            );
                          }
                        } else {
                          // Handle password mismatch
                          ScaffoldMessenger.of(context).showSnackBar(
                            SnackBar(content: Text('Passwords do not match')),
                          );
                        }
                      },
                      child: Container(
                        width: double.infinity,
                        height: 57,
                        decoration: ShapeDecoration(
                          color: Color(0xFF007AFF), // Original button color
                          shape: RoundedRectangleBorder(
                            borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(13),
                          ),
                        ),
                        child: Center(
                          child: Text(
                            'SIGN UP',
                            style: TextStyle(
                              color: Colors.white,
                              fontSize: 16,
                              fontFamily: 'Inter',
                              fontWeight: FontWeight.w700,
                            ),
                          ),
                        ),
                      ),
                    ),
                    SizedBox(height: 40), // Space at the bottom
                  ],
                ),
              ),
            ),
          ],
        ),
      ),
    );
  }

  Widget _buildInputField({
    required TextEditingController controller,
    required String icon,
    required String placeholder,
    required bool isPassword,
    bool isVisible = false,
    Function()? toggleVisibility,
  }) {
    return Container(
      width: double.infinity,
      height: 57,
      padding: EdgeInsets.symmetric(horizontal: 10),
      decoration: ShapeDecoration(
        color: Colors.white.withOpacity(0.2), // Semi-transparent background for input fields
        shape: RoundedRectangleBorder(
          side: BorderSide(width: 1, color: Colors.white), // White border for input fields
          borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(13),
        ),
      ),
      child: Row(
        children: [
          Image.asset(icon, width: 20, height: 20),
          SizedBox(width: 10),
          Expanded(
            child: TextField(
              controller: controller,
              obscureText: isPassword && !isVisible,
              style: TextStyle(color: Colors.black),
              decoration: InputDecoration(
                hintText: placeholder,
                hintStyle: TextStyle(color: Colors.black),
                border: InputBorder.none,
              ),
            ),
          ),
          if (isPassword)
            IconButton(
              icon: Icon(
                isVisible ? Icons.visibility : Icons.visibility_off,
                color: Colors.black,
              ),
              onPressed: toggleVisibility,
            ),
        ],
      ),
    );
  }
}

import 'home.dart'; // Import your HomePage
import 'forgot_password.dart'; // Import your ForgotPasswordPage
import 'Sign_up.dart'; // Import your SignUpPage
import 'package:firebase_auth/firebase_auth.dart';

class LogInPage extends StatefulWidget {
  @override
  _LogInPageState createState() => _LogInPageState();
}

class _LogInPageState extends State<LogInPage> {
  bool _isObscuredPassword = true;
  final TextEditingController _emailController = TextEditingController();
  final TextEditingController _passwordController = TextEditingController();
  final FirebaseAuth _auth = FirebaseAuth.instance;

  // Function to handle login
  Future<void> _login() async {
    try {
      await _auth.signInWithEmailAndPassword(
        email: _emailController.text.trim(),
        password: _passwordController.text.trim(),
      );
      // Navigate to HomePage on successful login
      Navigator.pushReplacement(
        context,
        MaterialPageRoute(builder: (context) => HomePage()),
      );
    } catch (e) {
      String errorMessage;
      // Custom error messages based on the exception
      if (e is FirebaseAuthException) {
        switch (e.code) {
          case 'user-not-found':
            errorMessage = 'No user found with this email.';
            break;
          case 'wrong-password':
            errorMessage = 'Incorrect password. Please try again.';
            break;
          default:
            errorMessage = 'Login failed. Please try again.';
            break;
        }
      } else {
        errorMessage = 'An unexpected error occurred. Please try again.';
      }
      // Show error message in a dialog
      _showErrorDialog(errorMessage);
    }
  }

  // Function to display error message
  void _showErrorDialog(String message) {
    showDialog(
      context: context,
      builder: (ctx) => AlertDialog(
        title: Text('Login Failed'),
        content: Text(message),
        actions: [
          TextButton(
            onPressed: () {
              Navigator.of(ctx).pop();
            },
            child: Text('Okay'),
          ),
        ],
      ),
    );
  }

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return Scaffold(
      body: Container(
        decoration: const BoxDecoration(
          gradient: LinearGradient(
            begin: Alignment.topCenter,
            end: Alignment.bottomCenter,
            colors: [Color(0xFF107AED), Color(0xFFB9D7F6)],
          ),
        ),
        child: SafeArea(
          child: SingleChildScrollView(
            child: Padding(
              padding: const EdgeInsets.symmetric(horizontal: 20.0),
              child: Column(
                crossAxisAlignment: CrossAxisAlignment.stretch,
                children: [
                  SizedBox(height: 50), // Adds space at the top
                  Center(
                    child: Image.asset(
                      'assets/images/logo1.png', // Adjust your logo path
                      width: 200,
                      height: 200,
                      fit: BoxFit.contain,
                    ),
                  ),
                  SizedBox(height: 50),
                  Text(
                    'LOGIN',
                    style: TextStyle(
                      fontSize: 32,
                      fontWeight: FontWeight.bold,
                      color: Colors.black,
                    ),
                    textAlign: TextAlign.center,
                  ),
                  SizedBox(height: 40),
                  // Email Field
                  Container(
                    decoration: BoxDecoration(
                      color: Color(0x007B7B7B),
                      borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(13),
                      border: Border.all(color: Colors.black, width: 1),
                    ),
                    child: TextField(
                      controller: _emailController,
                      decoration: InputDecoration(
                        prefixIcon: Icon(Icons.person, color: Colors.black),
                        hintText: 'Enter Email',
                        hintStyle: TextStyle(color: Color(0xFF424242)),
                        border: InputBorder.none,
                      ),
                    ),
                  ),
                  SizedBox(height: 20),
                  // Password Field
                  Container(
                    decoration: BoxDecoration(
                      color: Color(0x007B7B7B),
                      borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(13),
                      border: Border.all(color: Colors.black, width: 1),
                    ),
                    child: TextField(
                      controller: _passwordController,
                      obscureText: _isObscuredPassword,
                      decoration: InputDecoration(
                        prefixIcon: Icon(Icons.lock, color: Colors.black),
                        hintText: 'Enter Password',
                        hintStyle: TextStyle(color: Color(0xFF424242)),
                        border: InputBorder.none,
                        suffixIcon: IconButton(
                          icon: Icon(
                            _isObscuredPassword ? Icons.visibility : Icons.visibility_off,
                            color: Colors.black,
                          ),
                          onPressed: () {
                            setState(() {
                              _isObscuredPassword = !_isObscuredPassword;
                            });
                          },
                        ),
                      ),
                    ),
                  ),
                  SizedBox(height: 20),
                  // Login Button
                  GestureDetector(
                    onTap: _login, // Call the login function here
                    child: Container(
                      height: 57,
                      decoration: BoxDecoration(
                        color: Color(0xFF007AFF),
                        borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(13),
                      ),
                      child: Center(
                        child: Text(
                          'LOG IN',
                          style: TextStyle(
                            color: Colors.white,
                            fontSize: 16,
                            fontWeight: FontWeight.bold,
                          ),
                        ),
                      ),
                    ),
                  ),
                  SizedBox(height: 20),
                  // Forgot Password
                  TextButton(
                    onPressed: () {
                      // Navigate to ForgotPasswordPage
                      Navigator.push(
                        context,
                        MaterialPageRoute(builder: (context) => ForgotPasswordPage()),
                      );
                    },
                    child: Text(
                      'Forgot password?',
                      style: TextStyle(color: Color(0xFF007AFF)),
                    ),
                  ),
                  SizedBox(height: 10),
                  // Sign Up
                  Row(
                    mainAxisAlignment: MainAxisAlignment.center,
                    children: [
                      Text('Donâ€™t have an account?', style: TextStyle(color: Colors.black)),
                      TextButton(
                        onPressed: () {
                          // Navigate to SignUpPage

                          );
                        },
                        child: Text(
                          'Sign up',
                          style: TextStyle(color: Color(0xFF007AFF)),
                        ),

login.dart
01/11/2024, 21:37 - KilllerrrrrğŸ¦‹â¤ï¸â€ğŸ©¹: import 'package:firebase_auth/firebase_auth.dart';
import 'package:firebase_core/firebase_core.dart';
import 'package:flutter/material.dart';
import 'sign_up.dart';
import 'login.dart';
import 'entry.dart';
import 'forgot_password.dart';
import 'verification.dart';
import 'change_password.dart';
import 'password_changed.dart';
import 'home.dart';
import 'firebase_options.dart'; // Import your Firebase options

void main() async {
  WidgetsFlutterBinding.ensureInitialized();
  await Firebase.initializeApp(options: DefaultFirebaseOptions.currentPlatform);

  runApp(const FigmaToCodeApp());
}

class FigmaToCodeApp extends StatelessWidget {
  const FigmaToCodeApp({super.key});

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return MaterialApp(
      debugShowCheckedModeBanner: false,
      theme: ThemeData.dark().copyWith(
        scaffoldBackgroundColor: const Color.fromARGB(255, 18, 32, 47),
      ),
      home: StreamBuilder<User?>(
        stream: FirebaseAuth.instance.authStateChanges(),
        builder: (context, snapshot) {
          if (snapshot.connectionState == ConnectionState.waiting) {
            return Center(child: CircularProgressIndicator());
          }
          if (snapshot.hasError) {
            print("Error: ${snapshot.error}"); // Debug error
            return Center(child: Text("Something went wrong!"));
          }
          if (snapshot.hasData) {
            print("User is logged in: ${snapshot.data}"); // Debug user
            return HomePage(); // Navigate to HomePage if authenticated
          }
          print("User is not logged in"); // Debug no user
          return EntryPage(); // Navigate to EntryPage if not authenticated
        },
      ),
      routes: {
        '/login': (context) => LogInPage(),
        '/forgot_password': (context) => ForgotPasswordPage(),
        // Updated route to include verificationId as a parameter
        '/verification': (context) => VerificationPage(verificationId: ModalRoute.of(context)!.settings.arguments as String),
        '/change_password': (context) => ChangePasswordPage(),
        '/password_changed': (context) => ChangedPasswordPage(),
        '/sign_up': (context) => SignUpPage(),
      },
    );
  }
}

void main() async {
  WidgetsFlutterBinding.ensureInitialized();
  await Firebase.initializeApp(options: DefaultFirebaseOptions.currentPlatform);

  runApp(const FigmaToCodeApp());
}

class FigmaToCodeApp extends StatelessWidget {
  const FigmaToCodeApp({super.key});

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return MaterialApp(
      debugShowCheckedModeBanner: false,
      theme: ThemeData.dark().copyWith(
        scaffoldBackgroundColor: const Color.fromARGB(255, 18, 32, 47),
      ),
      home: StreamBuilder<User?>(
        stream: FirebaseAuth.instance.authStateChanges(),
        builder: (context, snapshot) {
          if (snapshot.connectionState == ConnectionState.waiting) {
            return Center(child: CircularProgressIndicator());
          }
          if (snapshot.hasError) {
            print("Error: ${snapshot.error}"); // Debug error
            return Center(child: Text("Something went wrong!"));
          }
          if (snapshot.hasData) {
            print("User is logged in: ${snapshot.data}"); // Debug user
            return HomePage(); // Navigate to HomePage if authenticated
          }
          print("User is not logged in"); // Debug no user
          return EntryPage(); // Navigate to EntryPage if not authenticated
        },
      ),
      routes: {
        '/login': (context) => LogInPage(),
        '/forgot_password': (context) => ForgotPasswordPage(),
        // Updated route to include verificationId as a parameter
        '/verification': (context) => VerificationPage(verificationId: ModalRoute.of(context)!.settings.arguments as String),
        '/change_password': (context) => ChangePasswordPage(),
        '/password_changed': (context) => ChangedPasswordPage(),
        '/sign_up': (context) => SignUpPage(),
      },
    );
  }
}

06/11/2024, 22:06 - KilllerrrrrğŸ¦‹â¤ï¸â€ğŸ©¹: import 'package:flutter/material.dart';
import 'home.dart'; // Import your HomePage
import 'forgot_password.dart'; // Import your ForgotPasswordPage
import 'Sign_up.dart'; // Import your SignUpPage
import 'package:firebase_auth/firebase_auth.dart';

class LogInPage extends StatefulWidget {
  @override
  _LogInPageState createState() => _LogInPageState();
}

class _LogInPageState extends State<LogInPage> {
  bool _isObscuredPassword = true;
  final TextEditingController _emailController = TextEditingController();
  final TextEditingController _passwordController = TextEditingController();
  final FirebaseAuth _auth = FirebaseAuth.instance;

  // Function to handle login
  Future<void> _login() async {
    try {
      await _auth.signInWithEmailAndPassword(
        email: _emailController.text.trim(),
        password: _passwordController.text.trim(),
      );
      // Navigate to HomePage on successful login
      Navigator.pushReplacement(
        context,
        MaterialPageRoute(builder: (context) => HomePage()),
      );
    } catch (e) {
      String errorMessage;
      // Custom error messages based on the exception
      if (e is FirebaseAuthException) {
        switch (e.code) {
          case 'user-not-found':
            errorMessage = 'No user found with this email.';
            break;
          case 'wrong-password':
            errorMessage = 'Incorrect password. Please try again.';
            break;
          default:
            errorMessage = 'Login failed. Please try again.';
            break;
        }
      } else {
        errorMessage = 'An unexpected error occurred. Please try again.';
      }
      // Show error message in a dialog
      _showErrorDialog(errorMessage);
    }
  }

  // Function to display error message
  void _showErrorDialog(String message) {
    showDialog(
      context: context,
      builder: (ctx) => AlertDialog(
        title: Text('Login Failed'),
        content: Text(message),
        actions: [
          TextButton(
            onPressed: () {
              Navigator.of(ctx).pop();
            },
            child: Text('Okay'),
          ),
        ],
      ),
    );
  }

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return Scaffold(
      body: Container(
        decoration: const BoxDecoration(
          gradient: LinearGradient(
            begin: Alignment.topCenter,
            end: Alignment.bottomCenter,
            colors: [Color(0xFF107AED), Color(0xFFB9D7F6)],
          ),
        ),
        child: SafeArea(
          child: SingleChildScrollView(
            child: Padding(
              padding: const EdgeInsets.symmetric(horizontal: 20.0),
              child: Column(
                crossAxisAlignment: CrossAxisAlignment.stretch,
                children: [
                  SizedBox(height: 50), // Adds space at the top

                  SizedBox(height: 40),
                  // Email Field
                  Container(

                      borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(13),
                      border: Border.all(color: Colors.black, width: 1),
                    ),
                    child: TextField(

                      decoration: InputDecoration(

import 'home.dart'; // Import your HomePage
import 'package:firebase_auth/firebase_auth.dart';

class SignUpPage extends StatefulWidget {
  @override
  _SignUpPageState createState() => _SignUpPageState();
}

class _SignUpPageState extends State<SignUpPage> {
  final TextEditingController _employeeIdController = TextEditingController();
  final TextEditingController _emailController = TextEditingController();
  final TextEditingController _passwordController = TextEditingController();
  final TextEditingController _confirmPasswordController = TextEditingController();

  bool _isPasswordVisible = false;
  bool _isConfirmPasswordVisible = false;

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return Scaffold(
      backgroundColor: const Color(0xFFB9D7F6), // Background color gradient end
      body: SingleChildScrollView(
        child: Column(
          children: [
            Container(
              width: double.infinity,
              height: 846,
              decoration: BoxDecoration(
                gradient: LinearGradient(
                  begin: Alignment(0.00, -1.00),
                  end: Alignment(0, 1),
                  colors: [Color(0xFF107AED), Color(0xFFB9D7F6)], // Gradient from the original
                ),
                borderRadius: BorderRadius.only(
                  bottomLeft: Radius.circular(40),
                  bottomRight: Radius.circular(40),
                ),
              ),
              child: Padding(
                padding: const EdgeInsets.symmetric(horizontal: 34.0), // Use consistent padding
                child: Column(
                  children: [
                    SizedBox(height: 135), // Space from the top
                    // Logo Placeholder Image
                    Container(
                      width: 165,
                      height: 145,
                      decoration: BoxDecoration(
                        image: DecorationImage(
                          image: AssetImage("assets/images/logo1.png"),
                          fit: BoxFit.cover,
                        ),
                      ),
                    ),
                    SizedBox(height: 20),
                    // Sign Up Text
                    Text(
                      'SIGN UP',
                      style: TextStyle(
                        color: Colors.black,
                        fontSize: 32,
                        fontFamily: 'Roboto',
                        fontWeight: FontWeight.bold,
                        letterSpacing: 1.5,
                      ),
                    ),
                    SizedBox(height: 40),
                    // Employee ID input field
                    _buildInputField(
                      controller: _employeeIdController,
                      icon: "assets/images/Vector.png",
                      placeholder: 'EMPLOYEE ID',
                      isPassword: false,
                    ),
                    SizedBox(height: 20),
                    // Email input field
                    _buildInputField(
                      controller: _emailController,
                      icon: "assets/images/email.png",
                      placeholder: 'EMAIL',
                      isPassword: false,
                    ),
                    SizedBox(height: 20),
                    // Password input field
                    _buildInputField(
                      controller: _passwordController,
                      icon: "assets/images/lock.png",
                      placeholder: 'PASSWORD',
                      isPassword: true,
                      isVisible: _isPasswordVisible,
                      toggleVisibility: () {
                        setState(() {
                          _isPasswordVisible = !_isPasswordVisible;
                        });
                      },
                    ),
                    SizedBox(height: 20),
                    // Confirm Password input field
                    _buildInputField(
                      controller: _confirmPasswordController,
                      icon: "assets/images/lock.png",
                      placeholder: 'CONFIRM PASSWORD',
                      isPassword: true,
                      isVisible: _isConfirmPasswordVisible,
                      toggleVisibility: () {
                        setState(() {
                          _isConfirmPasswordVisible = !_isConfirmPasswordVisible;
                        });
                      },
                    ),
                    SizedBox(height: 40), // Space before the button
                    // Sign Up button
                    GestureDetector(
                      onTap: () async {
                        if (_passwordController.text.trim() ==
                            _confirmPasswordController.text.trim()) {
                          try {
                            // Create user with Firebase
                            UserCredential userCredential = await FirebaseAuth.instance.createUserWithEmailAndPassword(
                              email: _emailController.text.trim(),
                              password: _passwordController.text.trim(),
                            );
                            // Navigate to HomePage
                            Navigator.pushReplacement(
                              context,
                              MaterialPageRoute(builder: (context) => HomePage()),
                            );
                          } on FirebaseAuthException catch (e) {
                            // Handle error
                            ScaffoldMessenger.of(context).showSnackBar(
                              SnackBar(content: Text(e.message ?? 'Sign up failed')),
                            );
                          }
                        } else {
                          // Handle password mismatch
                          ScaffoldMessenger.of(context).showSnackBar(
                            SnackBar(content: Text('Passwords do not match')),
                          );
                        }
                      },
                      child: Container(
                        width: double.infinity,
                        height: 57,
                        decoration: ShapeDecoration(
                          color: Color(0xFF007AFF), // Original button color
                          shape: RoundedRectangleBorder(
                            borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(13),
                          ),
                        ),
                        child: Center(
                          child: Text(
                            'SIGN UP',
                            style: TextStyle(
                              color: Colors.white,
                              fontSize: 16,
                              fontFamily: 'Inter',
                              fontWeight: FontWeight.w700,
                            ),
                          ),
                        ),
                      ),
                    ),
                    SizedBox(height: 40), // Space at the bottom
                  ],
                ),
              ),
            ),
          ],
        ),
      ),
    );
  }

  Widget _buildInputField({
    required TextEditingController controller,
    required String icon,
    required String placeholder,
    required bool isPassword,
    bool isVisible = false,
    Function()? toggleVisibility,
  }) {
    return Container(
      width: double.infinity,
      height: 57,
      padding: EdgeInsets.symmetric(horizontal: 10),
      decoration: ShapeDecoration(
        color: Colors.white.withOpacity(0.2), // Semi-transparent background for input fields
        shape: RoundedRectangleBorder(
          side: BorderSide(width: 1, color: Colors.white), // White border for input fields
          borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(13),
        ),
      ),
      child: Row(
        children: [
          Image.asset(icon, width: 20, height: 20),
          SizedBox(width: 10),
          Expanded(
            child: TextField(
              controller: controller,
              obscureText: isPassword && !isVisible,
              style: TextStyle(color: Colors.black),
              decoration: InputDecoration(
                hintText: placeholder,
                hintStyle: TextStyle(color: Colors.black),
                border: InputBorder.none,
              ),
            ),
          ),
          if (isPassword)
            IconButton(
              icon: Icon(
                isVisible ? Icons.visibility : Icons.visibility_off,
                color: Colors.black,
              ),
              onPressed: toggleVisibility,
            ),
        ],
      ),
    );
  }
}

09/12/2024, 00:04 - KilllerrrrrğŸ¦‹â¤ï¸â€ğŸ©¹: I can create a flow diagram for you. Since I don't have direct access to tools like Whimsical, I can design the structure here and give you instructions to create it in tools like **Whimsical**, **Lucidchart**, **Canva**, or even Google Drawings.

### **Flow Diagram Description: Medical Recommendation System**

**1. Input Layer (User Interface)**  
   - Users input symptoms via the web application.

**2. Preprocessing Layer (Backend)**  
   - Symptoms are encoded into machine-readable formats.

**3. Prediction Layer (Machine Learning)**  
   - The **Support Vector Classifier (SVC)** processes the data and predicts the disease.

**4. Recommendation Layer (Database)**  
   - Retrieves associated treatments, medications, precautions, and diets from the database.

**5. Output Layer (User Interface)**  
   - Displays disease prediction and holistic health recommendations.

12/12/2024, 22:56 - KilllerrrrrğŸ¦‹â¤ï¸â€ğŸ©¹: import 'package:flutter/material.dart';
import 'package:firebase_auth/firebase_auth.dart'; // Assuming Firebase for authentication
import 'package:cloud_firestore/cloud_firestore.dart';

void main() {
  runApp(MyApp());
}

class MyApp extends StatelessWidget {
  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return MaterialApp(
      debugShowCheckedModeBanner: false,
      title: 'Admin Dashboard',
      theme: ThemeData(
        primarySwatch: Colors.blue,
      ),
      home: AdminLoginPage(),
    );
  }
}

// Admin Login Page (for authentication)
class AdminLoginPage extends StatefulWidget {
  @override
  _AdminLoginPageState createState() => _AdminLoginPageState();
}

class _AdminLoginPageState extends State<AdminLoginPage> {
  final TextEditingController _passcodeController = TextEditingController();
  final FirebaseAuth _auth = FirebaseAuth.instance;

  // Function to handle admin login
  void _login() async {
    String passcode = _passcodeController.text;

    if (passcode == 'admin123') {
      // Successful login
      Navigator.pushReplacement(
        context,
        MaterialPageRoute(builder: (context) => AdminDashboard()),
      );
    } else {
      // Show error for incorrect passcode
      ScaffoldMessenger.of(context).showSnackBar(
        SnackBar(content: Text('Incorrect passcode!')),
      );
    }
  }

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return Scaffold(
      appBar: AppBar(title: Text('Admin Login')),
      body: Padding(
        padding: const EdgeInsets.all(16.0),
        child: Column(
          children: [
            TextField(
              controller: _passcodeController,
              decoration: InputDecoration(labelText: 'Enter Passcode'),
              obscureText: true,
            ),
            SizedBox(height: 20),
            ElevatedButton(
              onPressed: _login,
              child: Text('Login'),
            ),
          ],
        ),
      ),
    );
  }
}

// Admin Dashboard Page
class AdminDashboard extends StatelessWidget {
  final List<String> machines = [
    'Overhead Drilling Machine',
    'CNC Machine',
    'Grinding Machine',
    'Hydraulic Press Machine',
    'Injection Molding Machine'
  ];
  final List<String> shifts = ['Morning', 'Afternoon', 'Evening'];

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return Scaffold(
      appBar: AppBar(
        title: Text('Admin Dashboard'),
        actions: [
          IconButton(
            icon: Icon(Icons.logout),
            onPressed: () {
              FirebaseAuth.instance.signOut(); // Sign out admin
              Navigator.pushReplacement(
                context,
                MaterialPageRoute(builder: (context) => AdminLoginPage()),
              );
            },
          ),
        ],
      ),
      body: Padding(
        padding: const EdgeInsets.all(16.0),
        child: Column(
          children: [
            // User Status Section
            Expanded(
              child: StreamBuilder(
                stream: FirebaseFirestore.instance
                    .collection('users') // Firebase collection for users
                    .snapshots(),
                builder: (context, snapshot) {
                  if (snapshot.connectionState == ConnectionState.waiting) {
                    return Center(child: CircularProgressIndicator());
                  }

                  if (!snapshot.hasData || snapshot.data!.docs.isEmpty) {
                    return Center(child: Text('No users found'));
                  }

                  var users = snapshot.data!.docs;

                  return ListView.builder(
                    itemCount: users.length,
                    itemBuilder: (context, index) {
                      var user = users[index];
                      return Card(
                        margin: EdgeInsets.symmetric(vertical: 8),
                        child: ListTile(
                          title: Text(user['name']),
                          subtitle: Text('Status: ${user['status']}'),
                          trailing: IconButton(
                            icon: Icon(Icons.edit),
                            onPressed: () {
                              _showUserAssignmentDialog(context, user);
                            },
                          ),
                        ),
                      );
                    },
                  );
                },
              ),
            ),
          ],
        ),
      ),
    );
  }

  // Function to show dialog to assign machines and shifts to user
  void _showUserAssignmentDialog(BuildContext context, user) {
    final _machineController = TextEditingController();
    final _shiftController = TextEditingController();

    showDialog(
      context: context,
      builder: (context) {
        return AlertDialog(
          title: Text('Assign User: ${user['name']}'),
          content: Column(
            mainAxisSize: MainAxisSize.min,
            children: [
              DropdownButtonFormField<String>(
                decoration: InputDecoration(labelText: 'Select Machine'),
                items: machines
                    .map((machine) => DropdownMenuItem(
                        value: machine, child: Text(machine)))
                    .toList(),
                onChanged: (value) {
                  _machineController.text = value ?? '';
                },
              ),
              DropdownButtonFormField<String>(
                decoration: InputDecoration(labelText: 'Select Shift'),
                items: shifts
                    .map((shift) => DropdownMenuItem(
                        value: shift, child: Text(shift)))
                    .toList(),
                onChanged: (value) {
                  _shiftController.text = value ?? '';
                },
              ),
            ],
          ),
          actions: [
            TextButton(
              onPressed: () {
                Navigator.pop(context); // Close dialog
              },
              child: Text('Cancel'),
            ),
            TextButton(
              onPressed: () {
                // Update user with new machine and shift
                FirebaseFirestore.instance
                    .collection('users')
                    .doc(user.id)
                    .update({
                  'machine': _machineController.text,
                  'shift': _shiftController.text,
                  'status': 'Active', // Update status to Active
                });

                Navigator.pop(context); // Close dialog
              },
              child: Text('Save'),
            ),
          ],
        );
      },
    );
  }
}

class MyApp extends StatelessWidget {

class AdminDashboard extends StatelessWidget {
  final List<String> machines = [
    'Overhead Drilling Machine',
    'CNC Machine',
    'Grinding Machine',
    'Hydraulic Press Machine',
    'Injection Molding Machine'
  ];
  final List<String> shifts = ['Morning', 'Afternoon', 'Evening'];

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return Scaffold(
      appBar: AppBar(
        title: Text('Admin Dashboard'),
        actions: [
          IconButton(
            icon: Icon(Icons.logout),
            onPressed: () {
              // Implement logout functionality if necessary
              Navigator.pushReplacementNamed(context, '/login');
            },
          ),
        ],
      ),
      body: Padding(
        padding: const EdgeInsets.all(16.0),
        child: Column(
          children: [
            // User Status Section
            Expanded(
              child: StreamBuilder(
                stream: FirebaseFirestore.instance
                    .collection('users') // Firebase collection for users
                    .snapshots(),
                builder: (context, snapshot) {
                  if (snapshot.connectionState == ConnectionState.waiting) {
                    return Center(child: CircularProgressIndicator());
                  }

                  if (!snapshot.hasData || snapshot.data!.docs.isEmpty) {
                    return Center(child: Text('No users found'));
                  }

                  var users = snapshot.data!.docs;

                  return ListView.builder(
                    itemCount: users.length,
                    itemBuilder: (context, index) {
                      var user = users[index];
                      return Card(
                        margin: EdgeInsets.symmetric(vertical: 8),
                        child: ListTile(
                          title: Text(user['name']),
                          subtitle: Text('Status: ${user['status']}'),
                          trailing: IconButton(
                            icon: Icon(Icons.edit),
                            onPressed: () {
                              _showUserAssignmentDialog(context, user);
                            },
                          ),
                        ),
                      );
                    },
                  );
                },
              ),
            ),
          ],
        ),
      ),
    );
  }

  // Function to show dialog to assign machines and shifts to user
  void _showUserAssignmentDialog(BuildContext context, user) {
    final _machineController = TextEditingController();
    final _shiftController = TextEditingController();

    showDialog(
      context: context,
      builder: (context) {
        return AlertDialog(
          title: Text('Assign User: ${user['name']}'),
          content: Column(
            mainAxisSize: MainAxisSize.min,
            children: [
              DropdownButtonFormField<String>(
                decoration: InputDecoration(labelText: 'Select Machine'),
                items: machines
                    .map((machine) => DropdownMenuItem(
                        value: machine, child: Text(machine)))
                    .toList(),
                onChanged: (value) {
                  _machineController.text = value ?? '';
                },
              ),
              DropdownButtonFormField<String>(
                decoration: InputDecoration(labelText: 'Select Shift'),
                items: shifts
                    .map((shift) => DropdownMenuItem(
                        value: shift, child: Text(shift)))
                    .toList(),
                onChanged: (value) {
                  _shiftController.text = value ?? '';
                },
              ),
            ],
          ),
          actions: [
            TextButton(
              onPressed: () {
                Navigator.pop(context); // Close dialog
              },
              child: Text('Cancel'),
            ),
            TextButton(
              onPressed: () {
                // Update user with new machine and shift
                FirebaseFirestore.instance
                    .collection('users')
                    .doc(user.id)
                    .update({
                  'machine': _machineController.text,
                  'shift': _shiftController.text,
                  'status': 'Active', // Update status to Active
                });

                Navigator.pop(context); // Close dialog
              },
              child: Text('Save'),
            ),
          ],
        );
      },
    );
  }
}

import 'package:pdf/widgets.dart' as pw;
import 'package:pdf/pdf.dart';
import 'package:path_provider/path_provider.dart';
import 'dart:io';

import 'package:shared_preferences/shared_preferences.dart';

void main() {
  runApp(MyApp());
}

class MyApp extends StatelessWidget {
  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return MaterialApp(
      home: OHDReportPage(),
    );
  }
}

class OHDReportPage extends StatefulWidget {
  @override
  _OHDReportPageState createState() => _OHDReportPageState();
}

class _OHDReportPageState extends State<OHDReportPage> {
  final _formKey = GlobalKey<FormState>();

  // Controller for each input field
  final TextEditingController _machineController = TextEditingController();
  final TextEditingController _partNumberController = TextEditingController();
  final TextEditingController _productionCountController = TextEditingController();
  final TextEditingController _operatorNameController = TextEditingController();
  final TextEditingController _machineNumberController = TextEditingController();
  final TextEditingController _shiftController = TextEditingController();
  final TextEditingController _dateController = TextEditingController();
  final TextEditingController _spindleSpeedController = TextEditingController();
  final TextEditingController _drillBitDiameterController = TextEditingController();
  final TextEditingController _feedRateController = TextEditingController();
  final TextEditingController _holeDepthController = TextEditingController();
  final TextEditingController _coolantFlowRateController = TextEditingController();
  final TextEditingController _clampingPressureController = TextEditingController();

  // Function to save data using SharedPreferences
  Future<void> _saveData() async {
    final prefs = await SharedPreferences.getInstance();
    
    prefs.setString('machine', _machineController.text);
    prefs.setString('partNumber', _partNumberController.text);
    prefs.setString('productionCount', _productionCountController.text);
    prefs.setString('operatorName', _operatorNameController.text);
    prefs.setString('machineNumber', _machineNumberController.text);
    prefs.setString('shift', _shiftController.text);
    prefs.setString('date', _dateController.text);
    prefs.setString('spindleSpeed', _spindleSpeedController.text);
    prefs.setString('drillBitDiameter', _drillBitDiameterController.text);
    prefs.setString('feedRate', _feedRateController.text);
    prefs.setString('holeDepth', _holeDepthController.text);
    prefs.setString('coolantFlowRate', _coolantFlowRateController.text);
    prefs.setString('clampingPressure', _clampingPressureController.text);
    
    // Show a success message
    ScaffoldMessenger.of(context).showSnackBar(SnackBar(content: Text('Data Saved Successfully')));
  }

  // Function to generate the report from saved data
  Future<void> _generateReport() async {
    final prefs = await SharedPreferences.getInstance();
    
    // Retrieve the saved data
    final machineData = {
      'Machine': prefs.getString('machine') ?? '',
      'Part Number': prefs.getString('partNumber') ?? '',
      'Production Count': prefs.getString('productionCount') ?? '',
      'Operator Name': prefs.getString('operatorName') ?? '',
      'Machine Number': prefs.getString('machineNumber') ?? '',
      'Shift': prefs.getString('shift') ?? '',
      'Date': prefs.getString('date') ?? '',
      'Spindle Speed (RPM)': prefs.getString('spindleSpeed') ?? '',
      'Drill Bit Diameter (mm)': prefs.getString('drillBitDiameter') ?? '',
      'Feed Rate (mm/rev)': prefs.getString('feedRate') ?? '',
      'Hole Depth (mm)': prefs.getString('holeDepth') ?? '',
      'Coolant Flow Rate (L/min)': prefs.getString('coolantFlowRate') ?? '',
      'Clamping Pressure (Bar)': prefs.getString('clampingPressure') ?? '',
    };

    final pdf = pw.Document();

    // Add page
    pdf.addPage(pw.Page(build: (pw.Context context) {
      return pw.Column(
        children: [
          pw.Text("Overhead Drilling Machine Report", style: pw.TextStyle(fontSize: 18, fontWeight: pw.FontWeight.bold)),
          pw.SizedBox(height: 20),
          pw.Text("Machine Details:", style: pw.TextStyle(fontSize: 14, fontWeight: pw.FontWeight.bold)),
          pw.SizedBox(height: 10),
          pw.Table.fromTextArray(
            context: context,
            data: [
              ['Parameter', 'Value'],
              ...machineData.entries.map((entry) => [entry.key, entry.value]),
            ],
          ),
        ],
      );
    }));

    // Save PDF to file
    final output = await getTemporaryDirectory();
    final file = File("${output.path}/OHD_report_${prefs.getString('date')}.pdf");
    await file.writeAsBytes(await pdf.save());
    print('PDF saved to ${file.path}');

    // Share the PDF
    sharePdf(file.path);
  }

  // Share the generated PDF
  void sharePdf(String filePath) {
    Share.shareFiles([filePath], text: 'Overhead Drilling Machine Report');
  }

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return Scaffold(
      appBar: AppBar(
        title: Text('OHD Report Generator'),
      ),
      body: Padding(
        padding: EdgeInsets.all(16.0),
        child: Form(
          key: _formKey,
          child: Column(
            children: [
              TextFormField(
                controller: _machineController,
                decoration: InputDecoration(labelText: 'Machine Name'),
                validator: (value) => value!.isEmpty ? 'Please enter machine name' : null,
              ),
              TextFormField(
                controller: _partNumberController,
                decoration: InputDecoration(labelText: 'Part Number'),
                validator: (value) => value!.isEmpty ? 'Please enter part number' : null,
              ),
              TextFormField(
                controller: _productionCountController,
                decoration: InputDecoration(labelText: 'Production Count'),
                validator: (value) => value!.isEmpty ? 'Please enter production count' : null,
                keyboardType: TextInputType.number,
              ),
              TextFormField(
                controller: _operatorNameController,
                decoration: InputDecoration(labelText: 'Operator Name'),
              ),
              TextFormField(
                controller: _machineNumberController,
                decoration: InputDecoration(labelText: 'Machine Number'),
              ),
              TextFormField(
                controller: _shiftController,
                decoration: InputDecoration(labelText: 'Shift'),
              ),
              TextFormField(
                controller: _dateController,
                decoration: InputDecoration(labelText: 'Date'),
                validator: (value) => value!.isEmpty ? 'Please enter date' : null,
              ),
              // Add other fields similarly
              ElevatedButton(
                onPressed: () {
                  if (_formKey.currentState!.validate()) {
                    _saveData();
                  }
                },
                child: Text('Save Data'),
              ),
              ElevatedButton(
                onPressed: _generateReport,
                child: Text('Generate & Share Report'),
              ),
            ],
          ),
        ),
      ),
    );
  }
}
