import 'package:pdf/widgets.dart' as pw;
import 'dart:io';
import 'package:path_provider/path_provider.dart';

class ReportGenerator extends StatefulWidget {
  @override
  _ReportGeneratorState createState() => _ReportGeneratorState();
}

class _ReportGeneratorState extends State<ReportGenerator> {
  final TextEditingController _partNumberController = TextEditingController();
  final TextEditingController _productionCountController = TextEditingController();
  final TextEditingController _operatorNameController = TextEditingController();
  final TextEditingController _machineNumberController = TextEditingController();
  final TextEditingController _shiftController = TextEditingController();
  final TextEditingController _spindleSpeedController = TextEditingController();
  final TextEditingController _drillBitDiameterController = TextEditingController();
  final TextEditingController _feedRateController = TextEditingController();
  final TextEditingController _holeDepthController = TextEditingController();
  final TextEditingController _coolantFlowRateController = TextEditingController();
  final TextEditingController _clampingPressureController = TextEditingController();

  Future<void> _generatePDF() async {
    final pdf = pw.Document();

    pdf.addPage(
      pw.Page(
        build: (context) => pw.Column(
          crossAxisAlignment: pw.CrossAxisAlignment.start,
          children: [
            pw.Text('Overhead Drilling Machine (OHD) Report',
                style: pw.TextStyle(
                  fontSize: 18,
                  fontWeight: pw.FontWeight.bold,
                )),
            pw.SizedBox(height: 10),
            pw.Text('Part Number: ${_partNumberController.text}'),
            pw.Text('Production Count: ${_productionCountController.text}'),
            pw.Text('Operator Name: ${_operatorNameController.text}'),
            pw.Text('Machine Number: ${_machineNumberController.text}'),
            pw.Text('Shift: ${_shiftController.text}'),
            pw.Text('Spindle Speed (RPM): ${_spindleSpeedController.text}'),
            pw.Text('Drill Bit Diameter (mm): ${_drillBitDiameterController.text}'),
            pw.Text('Feed Rate (mm/rev): ${_feedRateController.text}'),
            pw.Text('Hole Depth (mm): ${_holeDepthController.text}'),
            pw.Text('Coolant Flow Rate (L/min): ${_coolantFlowRateController.text}'),
            pw.Text('Clamping Pressure (Bar): ${_clampingPressureController.text}'),
          ],
        ),
      ),
    );

    try {
      final output = await getApplicationDocumentsDirectory();
      final file = File("${output.path}/OHD_Report.pdf");
      await file.writeAsBytes(await pdf.save());

      ScaffoldMessenger.of(context).showSnackBar(
        SnackBar(content: Text('PDF generated at: ${file.path}')),
      );
    } catch (e) {
      ScaffoldMessenger.of(context).showSnackBar(
        SnackBar(content: Text('Failed to generate PDF: $e')),
      );
    }
  }

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return Scaffold(
      appBar: AppBar(
        title: Text('OHD Report Generator'),
      ),
      body: SingleChildScrollView(
        padding: EdgeInsets.all(16),
        child: Column(
          children: [
            TextField(
              controller: _partNumberController,
              decoration: InputDecoration(labelText: 'Part Number'),
            ),
            TextField(
              controller: _productionCountController,
              decoration: InputDecoration(labelText: 'Production Count'),
              keyboardType: TextInputType.number,
            ),
            TextField(

            ),

              decoration: InputDecoration(labelText: 'Machine Number'),
            ),
            TextField(
              controller: _shiftController,
              decoration: InputDecoration(labelText: 'Shift'),
            ),
            TextField(
              controller: _spindleSpeedController,
              decoration: InputDecoration(labelText: 'Spindle Speed (RPM)'),
              keyboardType: TextInputType.number,
            ),
            TextField(
              controller: _drillBitDiameterController,
              decoration: InputDecoration(labelText: 'Drill Bit Diameter (mm)'),
              keyboardType: TextInputType.number,
            ),
            TextField(
              controller: _feedRateController,
              decoration: InputDecoration(labelText: 'Feed Rate (mm/rev)'),
              keyboardType: TextInputType.number,
            ),
            TextField(
              controller: _holeDepthController,
              decoration: InputDecoration(labelText: 'Hole Depth (mm)'),
              keyboardType: TextInputType.number,
            ),
            TextField(
              controller: _coolantFlowRateController,
              decoration: InputDecoration(labelText: 'Coolant Flow Rate (L/min)'),

            ),
            TextField(
              controller: _holeDepthController,
              decoration: InputDecoration(labelText: 'Hole Depth (mm)'),
              keyboardType: TextInputType.number,
            ),
            TextField(
              controller: _coolantFlowRateController,
              decoration: InputDecoration(labelText: 'Coolant Flow Rate (L/min)'),
              keyboardType: TextInputType.number,
            ),
            TextField(
              controller: _clampingPressureController,
              decoration: InputDecoration(labelText: 'Clamping Pressure (Bar)'),
              keyboardType: TextInputType.number,
            ),
            SizedBox(height: 20),
            ElevatedButton(
              onPressed: _generatePDF,
              child: Text('Generate PDF'),
            ),
          ],
        ),
      ),
    );
  }
}

void main() {
  runApp(MaterialApp(
    home: ReportGenerator(),
    debugShowCheckedModeBanner: false,
  ));

import 'package:firebase_database/firebase_database.dart';
import 'home.dart';
import 'Sign_up.dart';
import 'admin_dashboard.dart';
import 'forgot_password.dart';

class LoginPage extends StatefulWidget {
  const LoginPage({Key? key}) : super(key: key);

  @override
  _LoginPageState createState() => _LoginPageState();
}

class _LoginPageState extends State<LoginPage> {
  final _formKey = GlobalKey<FormState>();
  final TextEditingController _employeeIdController = TextEditingController();
  final TextEditingController _passwordController = TextEditingController();

  final DatabaseReference _database = FirebaseDatabase.instance.ref().child('users');

  void _login() {
    final employeeId = _employeeIdController.text;
    final password = _passwordController.text;

    // Admin check
    if (employeeId == 'admin' && password == 'Admin') {
      Navigator.pushReplacement(
        context,
        MaterialPageRoute(builder: (context) => const AdminHomePage()),
      );
      return;
    }

    // Regular user login
    _database.child(employeeId).get().then((snapshot) {
      if (snapshot.exists) {
        final data = snapshot.value as Map<dynamic, dynamic>;
        if (data['password'] == password) {
          Navigator.pushReplacement(
            context,
            MaterialPageRoute(builder: (context) => const HomePage()),
          );
        } else {
          ScaffoldMessenger.of(context).showSnackBar(
            const SnackBar(content: Text('Invalid password')),
          );
        }
      } else {
        ScaffoldMessenger.of(context).showSnackBar(
          const SnackBar(content: Text('User not found')),
        );
      }
    }).catchError((error) {
      ScaffoldMessenger.of(context).showSnackBar(
        SnackBar(content: Text('Error: $error')),
      );
    });
  }

  void _navigateToSignup() {
    Navigator.push(
      context,
      MaterialPageRoute(builder: (context) => const SignupPage()),
    );
  }

  void _navigateToForgotPassword() {
    Navigator.push(
      context,
      MaterialPageRoute(builder: (context) => const ForgotPasswordPage()),
    );
  }

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return Scaffold(
      body: Container(
        decoration: const BoxDecoration(
          gradient: LinearGradient(
            begin: Alignment.topCenter,
            end: Alignment.bottomCenter,
            colors: [Color(0xFF107AED), Color(0xFFB9D7F6)],
          ),
        ),
        child: SafeArea(
          child: SingleChildScrollView(
            child: Padding(
              padding: const EdgeInsets.symmetric(horizontal: 20.0),
              child: Column(
                crossAxisAlignment: CrossAxisAlignment.stretch,
                children: [
                  const SizedBox(height: 50),
                  Center(
                    child: Image.asset(
                      'assets/images/logo1.png',
                      width: 200,
                      height: 200,
                      fit: BoxFit.contain,
                    ),
                  ),
                  const SizedBox(height: 50),
                  const Text(
                    'LOGIN',
                    style: TextStyle(
                      fontSize: 32,
                      fontWeight: FontWeight.bold,
                      color: Colors.black,
                    ),
                    textAlign: TextAlign.center,
                  ),
                  const SizedBox(height: 40),
                  // Employee ID Field
                  Container(
                    decoration: BoxDecoration(
                      color: Colors.transparent,
                      borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(13),
                      border: Border.all(color: Colors.black, width: 1),
                    ),
                    child: TextFormField(

import 'package:firebase_database/firebase_database.dart';
import 'login.dart';

class SignupPage extends StatefulWidget {
  const SignupPage({Key? key}) : super(key: key);

  @override
  _SignupPageState createState() => _SignupPageState();
}

class _SignupPageState extends State<SignupPage> {
  final _formKey = GlobalKey<FormState>();
  final TextEditingController _employeeIdController = TextEditingController();
  final TextEditingController _nameController = TextEditingController();
  final TextEditingController _emailController = TextEditingController();
  final TextEditingController _passwordController = TextEditingController();
  final TextEditingController _confirmPasswordController = TextEditingController();

  final DatabaseReference _database = FirebaseDatabase.instance.ref().child('users');

  void _signup() {
    if (_formKey.currentState!.validate()) {
      final employeeId = _employeeIdController.text;
      final name = _nameController.text;
      final email = _emailController.text;
      final password = _passwordController.text;

      _database.child(employeeId).set({
        'employeeId': employeeId,
        'name': name,
        'email': email,
        'password': password,
      }).then((_) {
        ScaffoldMessenger.of(context).showSnackBar(
          const SnackBar(content: Text('Signup successful!')),
        );
        Navigator.pushReplacement(
          context,
          MaterialPageRoute(builder: (context) => const LoginPage()),
        );
      }).catchError((error) {
        ScaffoldMessenger.of(context).showSnackBar(
          SnackBar(content: Text('Error: $error')),
        );
      });
    }
  }

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return Scaffold(
      body: Container(

import 'package:cloud_firestore/cloud_firestore.dart';
import 'package:firebase_auth/firebase_auth.dart';

class AdminDashboard extends StatelessWidget {
  const AdminDashboard({Key? key}) : super(key: key);

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return Scaffold(
      appBar: AppBar(
        title: const Text('Admin Dashboard'),
        actions: [
          IconButton(
            icon: const Icon(Icons.logout),
            onPressed: () async {
              await FirebaseAuth.instance.signOut();
              Navigator.pop(context);
            },
          ),
        ],
      ),
      body: ListView(
        padding: const EdgeInsets.all(16.0),
        children: [
          ElevatedButton(
            onPressed: () {
              Navigator.push(
                context,
                MaterialPageRoute(builder: (context) => const UserAssignmentPage()),
              );
            },
            child: const Text('Assign Users to Machines'),
          ),
          ElevatedButton(
            onPressed: () {
              Navigator.push(
                context,
                MaterialPageRoute(builder: (context) => const MachineDetailsPage()),
              );
            },
            child: const Text('View Machine Details'),
          ),
        ],
      ),
    );
  }
}

class UserAssignmentPage extends StatefulWidget {
  const UserAssignmentPage({Key? key}) : super(key: key);

  @override
  _UserAssignmentPageState createState() => _UserAssignmentPageState();
}

class _UserAssignmentPageState extends State<UserAssignmentPage> {
  String? selectedMachine;
  String? selectedShift;
  final List<String> machines = ['Drilling', 'CNC', 'Grinding', 'Hydraulic', 'Injection'];
  final List<String> shifts = ['Morning', 'Evening', 'Night'];

  Future<void> saveAssignment() async {
    if (selectedMachine != null && selectedShift != null) {
      try {
        await FirebaseFirestore.instance.collection('assignments').add({
          'machine': selectedMachine,
          'shift': selectedShift,
          'timestamp': FieldValue.serverTimestamp(),
        });
        ScaffoldMessenger.of(context).showSnackBar(
          const SnackBar(content: Text('Assignment saved successfully!')),
        );
      } catch (e) {
        ScaffoldMessenger.of(context).showSnackBar(
          SnackBar(content: Text('Failed to save assignment: $e')),
        );
      }
    } else {
      ScaffoldMessenger.of(context).showSnackBar(
        const SnackBar(content: Text('Please select a machine and shift.')),
      );
    }
  }

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return Scaffold(
      appBar: AppBar(title: const Text('Assign Users to Machines')),
      body: Padding(
        padding: const EdgeInsets.all(16.0),
        child: Column(
          children: [
            DropdownButtonFormField<String>(
              value: selectedMachine,
              items: machines
                  .map((machine) => DropdownMenuItem(
                        value: machine,
                        child: Text(machine),
                      ))
                  .toList(),
              onChanged: (value) {
                setState(() {
                  selectedMachine = value;
                });
              },
              decoration: const InputDecoration(labelText: 'Select Machine'),
            ),
            const SizedBox(height: 16.0),
            DropdownButtonFormField<String>(
              value: selectedShift,
              items: shifts
                  .map((shift) => DropdownMenuItem(
                        value: shift,
                        child: Text(shift),
                      ))
                  .toList(),
              onChanged: (value) {
                setState(() {
                  selectedShift = value;
                });
              },
              decoration: const InputDecoration(labelText: 'Select Shift'),
            ),
            const SizedBox(height: 32.0),
            ElevatedButton(
              onPressed: saveAssignment,
              child: const Text('Save Assignment'),
            ),
          ],
        ),
      ),
    );
  }
}

class MachineDetailsPage extends StatelessWidget {
  const MachineDetailsPage({Key? key}) : super(key: key);

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return Scaffold(
      appBar: AppBar(title: const Text('Machine Details')),
      body: StreamBuilder<QuerySnapshot>(
        stream: FirebaseFirestore.instance.collection('machines').snapshots(),
        builder: (context, snapshot) {
          if (snapshot.connectionState == ConnectionState.waiting) {
            return const Center(child: CircularProgressIndicator());
          }
          if (snapshot.hasError) {
            return Center(child: Text('Error: ${snapshot.error}'));
          }
          final machines = snapshot.data?.docs ?? [];
          return ListView.builder(
            itemCount: machines.length,
            itemBuilder: (context, index) {
              final machine = machines[index];
              return ListTile(
                title: Text(machine['name'] ?? 'Unknown Machine'),
                subtitle: Text('Status: ${machine['status'] ?? 'Unknown'}'),
              );
            },
          );
        },
      ),
    );
  }
}

15/12/2024, 13:54 - KilllerrrrrğŸ¦‹â¤ï¸â€ğŸ©¹: Got it! Letâ€™s break it down step by step to ensure you're fully prepared:

---

### **Step 1: Understand the Job Roles and Expectations**
- **Roles offered**: Software Test Engineer, Full Stack Developer, Python Engineer, Data Analyst, DevOps Engineer.
- Focus on the **common skills** required across these roles:
  - **Programming**: Python, Java basics (focus on Python since you have experience).
  - **Problem-solving**: Data Structures & Algorithms.
  - **Database**: SQL queries and basic DBMS concepts.
  - **Tools**: For Data Analyst roles, review Power BI/Tableau basics.
  - **Aptitude**: Logical reasoning, quantitative aptitude, and verbal skills.

---

### **Step 2: Prepare for the Aptitude Test**
This is typically the first round and lasts for 60 minutes.

1. **Quantitative Aptitude**:  
   - Topics: Percentages, Ratios, Time & Work, Profit & Loss, Number Series, Simplifications.  
   - Practice: Use websites like IndiaBix or Aptitude test books.

2. **Logical Reasoning**:  
   - Topics: Puzzles, Blood Relations, Coding-Decoding, Syllogisms.  
   - Practice: Solve puzzles online or on apps like BrainBashers.

3. **Verbal Ability**:  
   - Topics: Grammar, Synonyms/Antonyms, Sentence Rearrangement, Reading Comprehension.  
   - Practice: Read short passages, review basic grammar rules.

---

### **Step 3: Prepare for Technical Topics**
1. **Programming** (Pick Python if you're more comfortable with it):
   - Revise: Loops, Functions, Classes, File Handling.
   - Practice: Write small programs on topics like Fibonacci series, sorting algorithms, and basic CRUD operations in Python.

2. **Data Structures & Algorithms**:
   - Revise: Arrays, Linked Lists, Stacks, Queues, Searching (Binary Search), Sorting (Bubble, Quick Sort), and basic recursion.
   - Practice: Solve easy-medium problems on **LeetCode** (since you already use it).

3. **Database**:
   - Focus: Basic SQL queries, Joins, Subqueries, Normalization, and basic ER diagrams.

4. **Testing Concepts** (For Software Test Engineer Role):
   - Revise: SDLC, STLC, Agile, Black Box Testing, and Test Cases.

5. **Domain-specific** (For Data Analyst or DevOps roles):
   - Data Analyst: Revise Excel formulas, Power BI basics, and simple visualizations.  
   - DevOps: Understand CI/CD, Docker basics, and version control (Git).

---

### **Step 4: Prepare for the Group Discussion (GD)**
1. **Common GD Topics**:
   - "Impact of AI on Employment."
   - "Cloud Computing: Future of IT."
   - "Does India need more startups?"
   - "Work from Home vs. Office."
2. **Tips**:
   - Speak clearly and confidently.
   - Structure your points: **Introduction, Main Points, Conclusion**.
   - Be respectful and listen to others.

---

### **Step 5: Pre-Placement Session**
1. Prepare to introduce yourself:
   - **Example**:  
     "Good morning, everyone. Iâ€™m Boomika M S, a final-year Information Science Engineering student at T. John Institute of Technology. Iâ€™ve completed internships in Python and Machine Learning, and Iâ€™ve worked on projects like hand gesture recognition and digitome app development. Iâ€™m passionate about coding and problem-solving, which drives me to continuously learn and improve my technical skills."

2. Highlight **strengths**: Problem-solving, adaptability, teamwork.

---

### **Step 6: Offer Round**
- Be prepared to discuss:
  - Your resume projects.
  - Why youâ€™re interested in the job role.
  - Long-term career goals.

---

### **Resources for Preparation**
1. **Coding Practice**: LeetCode, HackerRank.
2. **Aptitude Prep**: IndiaBix, RS Aggarwalâ€™s book.
3. **SQL**: W3Schools, SQLZoo.
4. **Technical Notes**: Revise your past project concepts.

---

What do you feel needs more focus? I can provide quick resources, mock questions, or tips on any specific area!
